</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A decorator</li>

***verslinden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verslinden.html>verslinden</a> (13609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verslinden.html>verslinden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*farslindan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fraslindaną</i>. 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verslinden.html>verslinden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to devour, to eat greedily</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verslinden.html>verslinden</a></b>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smal.html>smal</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>to narrow, narrow down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a> Kazan <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beroemdste.html>beroemdste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nauwste.html>nauwste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kloof.html>kloof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:traject.html>traject</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rivier.html>rivier</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:versmalt.html>versmalt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> 150 <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bereikt.html>bereikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepte.html>diepte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> 53 <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Great Kazan <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the most well known and the narrowest gorge of the route: the river here narrows down to 150 <a href = vnd.unilang:meters.html>meters</a> and reaches a depth of 53 <a href = vnd.unilang:meters.html>meters</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:versnellen.html>versnellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">accelerate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:versnelling.html>versnelling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:versnellingen.html>versnellingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:versnelling.html>versnellinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">acceleration</span> (act, state)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:versnijden.html>versnijden</a> (28415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">versniden</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">versnyden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:versnijden.html>versnijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut up, to cut in pieces</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destroy by cutting, to ruin by cutting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dilute, to mix, to adulterate, to step on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of old <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blend or mix (with younger <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">done to certain beers, like gueuze</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">overgankelijk</span> in <a href = vnd.unilang:stukken.html>stukken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a></li>

***verspillen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verspillen.html>verspillen</a> (3628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verspilden.html>verspilden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spil.html>spillen</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forspill</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verspillen.html>verspillen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to waste

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:aanvoegende.html>aanvoegende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstaan.html>verstaan</a></li></ol>

***verstaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstaan.html>verstaan</a> (2927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verstaen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">farstān</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fura</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stāną</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frastandaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to oppose; to understand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verstehen</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forstand</i>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">förstå</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verstaan.html>verstaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to understand (language, <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>), to hear clearly.</li>
<li>to understand (an idea), to comprehend</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In sense 2, the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrijpen.html>begrijpen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:verstaan.html>verstaan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">versteken</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> absence from a court meeting to which one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> summoned, default</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a joint formed by connecting two components at segments having 45° angles relative to their length or width, the whole forming a right angle</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstenen.html>verstenen</a> (55574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Petrified_tree_Kirstenbosch.jpg/220px-Petrified_tree_Kirstenbosch.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Petrified_tree_Kirstenbosch.jpg/330px-Petrified_tree_Kirstenbosch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Petrified_tree_Kirstenbosch.jpg/440px-Petrified_tree_Kirstenbosch.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Some <i><a href = vnd.unilang:versteend.html>versteend</a></i> (petrified) material</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verstênen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steen.html>steen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verstenen.html>verstenen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to petrify, turn (something) into rock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to harden, make insensitive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be petrified, <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> into rock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be hardened, to become rigid, implacable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to equip, fit (a mill) with a(nother) millstone</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stenen.html>stenen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to moan, complain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijf.html>stijf</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijven.html>stijven</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li>to stiffen, to become stiff, to freeze
